\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Derived$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base$<$ Derived $>$}
Base class for all dense matrices, vectors, and arrays. 

This class is the base that is inherited by all dense objects (matrix, vector, arrays, and related expression types). The common \doxylink{namespaceEigen}{Eigen} API for dense objects is contained in this class.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Derived} & is the derived type, e.\+g., a matrix type or an expression.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
This class can be extended with the help of the plugin mechanism described on the page Topic\+Customizing\+\_\+\+Plugins by defining the preprocessor symbol {\ttfamily EIGEN\+\_\+\+DENSEBASE\+\_\+\+PLUGIN}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\textbackslash{}blank Topic\+Class\+Hierarchy 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1conditional}{internal\+::conditional}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1is__same}{internal\+::is\+\_\+same}}$<$typenameinternal\+::traits$<$Derived$>$\+::\+Xpr\+Kind,\mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1MatrixXpr}{Matrix\+Xpr}}$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8da735a6bfc7012606acf787156d10a0}{\+::value}},\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aa301ef39d63443e9ef0b84f47350116e}{Plain\+Matrix}},\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a65328b7d6fc10a26ff6cd5801a6a44eb}{Plain\+Array}}$>$\+::type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Plain\+Object}



The plain matrix or array type corresponding to this expression. 

This is not necessarily exactly the return type of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()}. In the case of plain matrices, the return type of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} is a const reference to a matrix, not a matrix! It is however guaranteed that the return type of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} is either \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{Plain\+Object} or const \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{Plain\+Object}\&. \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!Scalar@{Scalar}}
\index{Scalar@{Scalar}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}

Size\+At\+Compile\+Time&This is equal to the number of coefficients, i.\+e. the number of rows times the number of columns, or to {\itshape Dynamic} if this is not known at compile-\/time. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dadb37c78ebbf15aa20b65c3b70415a1ab}{Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da787f85fd67ee5985917eb2cef6e70441}{Cols\+At\+Compile\+Time} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MaxRowsAtCompileTime@{MaxRowsAtCompileTime}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!MaxRowsAtCompileTime@{MaxRowsAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dad2baadea085372837b0e80dc93be1306}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dad2baadea085372837b0e80dc93be1306} 
Max\+Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time&This value is equal to the maximum possible number of rows that this expression might have. If this expression might have an arbitrarily high number of rows, this value is set to {\itshape Dynamic}.

This value is useful to know when evaluating an expression, in order to determine whether it is possible to avoid doing a dynamic memory allocation.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dadb37c78ebbf15aa20b65c3b70415a1ab}{Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dacc3a41000cf1d29dd1a320b2a09d2a65}{Max\+Cols\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da3a459062d39cb34452518f5f201161d2}{Max\+Size\+At\+Compile\+Time} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MaxColsAtCompileTime@{MaxColsAtCompileTime}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!MaxColsAtCompileTime@{MaxColsAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dacc3a41000cf1d29dd1a320b2a09d2a65}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dacc3a41000cf1d29dd1a320b2a09d2a65} 
Max\+Cols\+At\+Compile\+Time&This value is equal to the maximum possible number of columns that this expression might have. If this expression might have an arbitrarily high number of columns, this value is set to {\itshape Dynamic}.

This value is useful to know when evaluating an expression, in order to determine whether it is possible to avoid doing a dynamic memory allocation.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da787f85fd67ee5985917eb2cef6e70441}{Cols\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519dad2baadea085372837b0e80dc93be1306}{Max\+Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da3a459062d39cb34452518f5f201161d2}{Max\+Size\+At\+Compile\+Time} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MaxSizeAtCompileTime@{MaxSizeAtCompileTime}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!MaxSizeAtCompileTime@{MaxSizeAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da3a459062d39cb34452518f5f201161d2}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da3a459062d39cb34452518f5f201161d2} 
Max\+Size\+At\+Compile\+Time&This value is equal to the maximum possible number of coefficients that this expression might have. If this expression might have an arbitrarily high number of coefficients, this value is set to {\itshape Dynamic}.

This value is useful to know when evaluating an expression, in order to determine whether it is possible to avoid doing a dynamic memory allocation.

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{IsVectorAtCompileTime@{IsVectorAtCompileTime}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!IsVectorAtCompileTime@{IsVectorAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da1156955c8099c5072934b74c72654ed0}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da1156955c8099c5072934b74c72654ed0} 
Is\+Vector\+At\+Compile\+Time&This is set to true if either the number of rows or the number of columns is known at compile-\/time to be equal to 1. Indeed, in that case, we are dealing with a column-\/vector (if there is only one column) or with a row-\/vector (if there is only one row). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{NumDimensions@{NumDimensions}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!NumDimensions@{NumDimensions}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da4d4548a01ba37a6c2031a3c1f0a37d34}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da4d4548a01ba37a6c2031a3c1f0a37d34} 
Num\+Dimensions&This value is equal to Tensor\+::\+Num\+Dimensions, i.\+e. 0 for scalars, 1 for vectors, and 2 for matrices. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Flags@{Flags}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!Flags@{Flags}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da7392c9b2ad41ba3c16fdc5306c04d581}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da7392c9b2ad41ba3c16fdc5306c04d581} 
Flags&This stores expression \doxylink{group__flags}{Flags} flags which may or may not be inherited by new expressions constructed from this one. See the \doxylink{group__flags}{list of flags}. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{IsRowMajor@{IsRowMajor}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!IsRowMajor@{IsRowMajor}}}\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da406b6af91d61d348ba1c9764bdd66008}\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1c5061e6cfaa937b590e2d64b78a519da406b6af91d61d348ba1c9764bdd66008}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int NRows, int NCols$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ NRows, NCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a fixed-\/size expression of a block of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The template parameters {\itshape NRows} and {\itshape NCols} are the number of rows and columns in the block.

\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block\\

\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The usage of of this overload is discouraged from Eigen 3.\+4, better used the generic \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block(\+Index,\+Index,\+NRows\+Type,\+NCols\+Type)}, here is the one-\/to-\/one equivalence\+:

\end{DoxyCode}


since block is a templated member, the keyword template has to be used if the matrix type is also a template parameter\+:

\end{DoxyCode}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_adf40a0b66634af3002950c915ed15950}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!block@{block}}
\index{block@{block}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{block()}{block()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_adf40a0b66634af3002950c915ed15950} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int NRows, int NCols$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ NRows, NCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a block of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NRows} & number of rows in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em NCols} & number of columns in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em block\+Rows} & number of rows in block as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em block\+Cols} & number of columns in block as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for blocks where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape block\+Rows} should equal {\itshape NRows} unless {\itshape NRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The usage of of this overload is discouraged from Eigen 3.\+4, better used the generic \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block(\+Index,\+Index,\+NRows\+Type,\+NCols\+Type)}, here is the one-\/to-\/one complete equivalence\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{mat.template\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block<NRows,NCols>}}(i,j,rows,cols)\ \ \ \ \ <-\/-\/>\ \ mat.block(i,j,fix<NRows>(rows),fix<NCols>(cols))}

\end{DoxyCode}
 If we known that, e.\+g., NRows==Dynamic and NCols!=Dynamic, then the equivalence becomes\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{mat.template\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block<Dynamic,NCols>}}(i,j,rows,NCols)\ \ <-\/-\/>\ \ mat.block(i,j,rows,fix<NCols>)}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{block@{block}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename NRows\+Type, typename NCols\+Type$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NRows\+Type $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8da735a6bfc7012606acf787156d10a0}{\+::value}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NCols\+Type $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8da735a6bfc7012606acf787156d10a0}{\+::value}} $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{NRows\+Type}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{NCols\+Type}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a block in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em block\+Rows} & number of rows in the block, specified at either run-\/time or compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em block\+Cols} & number of columns in the block, specified at either run-\/time or compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NRows\+Type} & the type of the value handling the number of rows in the block, typically \doxylink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}. \\
\hline
{\em NCols\+Type} & the type of the value handling the number of columns in the block, typically \doxylink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
Example using runtime (aka dynamic) sizes\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\textbackslash{}newin\{3.\+4\}\+:

The number of rows {\itshape block\+Rows} and columns {\itshape block\+Cols} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. In the later case, {\ttfamily n} plays the role of a runtime fallback value in case {\ttfamily N} equals \doxylink{namespaceEigen_ad81fa7195215a0ce30017dfac309f0b2}{Eigen\+::\+Dynamic}. Here is an example with a fixed number of rows {\ttfamily NRows} and dynamic number of columns {\ttfamily cols\+:} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{mat.block(i,j,fix<NRows>,cols)}

\end{DoxyCode}


This function thus fully covers the features offered by the following overloads \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a20ca095fbf288a393066b0e08a504280}{block$<$\+NRows,\+NCols$>$(\+Index, Index)}, and \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_adf40a0b66634af3002950c915ed15950}{block$<$\+NRows,\+NCols$>$(\+Index, Index, Index, Index)} that are thus obsolete. Indeed, this generic version avoids redundancy, it preserves the argument order, and prevents the need to rely on the template keyword in templated code.

but with less redundancy and more consistency as it does not modify the argument order and seamlessly enable hybrid fixed/dynamic sizes.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size matrix, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
class \doxylink{classEigen_1_1Block}{Block}, fix, fix$<$\+N$>$(int) 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int CRows, int CCols$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::bottom\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a bottom-\/left corner of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1NRowsBlockXpr}{NRows\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NRows\+Type $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8da735a6bfc7012606acf787156d10a0}{\+::value}} $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::bottom\+Rows (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{NRows\+Type}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a block consisting of the bottom rows of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & the number of rows in the block \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NRows\+Type} & the type of the value handling the number of rows in the block, typically \doxylink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of rows {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block() } for the details. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a9053c1a2e9993febe50113b05aac0f20} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a constant matrix of value {\itshape value} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
This variant is only for fixed-\/size \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base} types. For dynamic-\/size types, you need to use the variants taking size arguments.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a0809dd2cb5b8f7dafcaa1083416beb8e}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!Constant@{Constant}}
\index{Constant@{Constant}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Constant()}{Constant()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a0809dd2cb5b8f7dafcaa1083416beb8e} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{cols}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a constant matrix of value {\itshape value} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

class \doxylink{classEigen_1_1CwiseNullaryOp}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ad8236107f739860be6a5debeede8fdbf}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!Constant@{Constant}}
\index{Constant@{Constant}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Constant()}{Constant()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ad8236107f739860be6a5debeede8fdbf} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{size}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a constant matrix of value {\itshape value} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameter {\itshape size} is the size of the returned vector. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base} type.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size vector types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape size} as argument, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

const version of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ae71d079e16d91360d10066b316b48485}{end()} \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!eval@{eval}}
\index{eval@{eval}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{eval()}{eval()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE Eval\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::eval (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the matrix or vector obtained by evaluating this expression.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Notice that in the case of a plain matrix or vector (not an expression) this function just returns a const reference, in order to avoid a useless copy.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Be careful with \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} and the auto C++ keyword, as detailed in this \doxylink{}{page }. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of coefficients {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block() } for the details.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the inner size.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For a vector, this is just the size. For a matrix (non-\/vector), this is the minor dimension with respect to the storage order, i.\+e., the number of rows for a column-\/major matrix, and the number of columns for a row-\/major matrix. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_af3793521d788a946cb9c5f4f92bab4d3}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isApprox@{isApprox}}
\index{isApprox@{isApprox}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isApprox()}{isApprox()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_af3793521d788a946cb9c5f4f92bab4d3} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC bool \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Approx (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Product}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1NumTraits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}}$>$\+:\+:dummy\+\_\+precision()}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is approximately equal to {\itshape other}, within the precision determined by {\itshape prec}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The fuzzy compares are done multiplicatively. Two vectors $ v $ and $ w $ are considered to be approximately equal within precision $ p $ if \[ \Vert v - w \Vert \leqslant p\,\min(\Vert v\Vert, \Vert w\Vert). \] For matrices, the comparison is done using the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm (aka Frobenius norm L2 norm).

Because of the multiplicativeness of this comparison, one can\textquotesingle{}t use this function to check whether {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is approximately equal to the zero matrix or vector. Indeed, {\ttfamily is\+Approx(zero)} returns false unless {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} itself is exactly the zero matrix or vector. If you want to test whether {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is zero, use internal\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than(const \+Real\+Scalar\&, Real\+Scalar) instead.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
internal\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than(const Real\+Scalar\&, Real\+Scalar) const 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aafb86c9868d3d9076e01e4fc54c93e81}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isApproxToConstant@{isApproxToConstant}}
\index{isApproxToConstant@{isApproxToConstant}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isApproxToConstant()}{isApproxToConstant()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aafb86c9868d3d9076e01e4fc54c93e81} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC bool \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Approx\+To\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Product}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1NumTraits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}}$>$\+:\+:dummy\+\_\+precision()}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if all coefficients in this matrix are approximately equal to {\itshape val}, to within precision {\itshape prec} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a800a25f323fc4222c822be5fdad729ac}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}}
\index{isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isMuchSmallerThan()}{isMuchSmallerThan()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a800a25f323fc4222c822be5fdad729ac} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC bool \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Product}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1NumTraits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}}$>$\+:\+:dummy\+\_\+precision()}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if the norm of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is much smaller than the norm of {\itshape other}, within the precision determined by {\itshape prec}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The fuzzy compares are done multiplicatively. A vector $ v $ is considered to be much smaller than a vector $ w $ within precision $ p $ if \[ \Vert v \Vert \leqslant p\,\Vert w\Vert. \] For matrices, the comparison is done using the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_af3793521d788a946cb9c5f4f92bab4d3}{is\+Approx()}, is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than(const Real\+Scalar\&, Real\+Scalar) const 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a43cb8e4cdd5908b18e50eb464dc67e3d}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}}
\index{isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isMuchSmallerThan()}{isMuchSmallerThan()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a43cb8e4cdd5908b18e50eb464dc67e3d} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC bool \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const typename \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1NumTraits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} $>$\+::\+Real \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Product}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if the norm of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is much smaller than {\itshape other}, within the precision determined by {\itshape prec}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The fuzzy compares are done multiplicatively. A vector $ v $ is considered to be much smaller than $ x $ within precision $ p $ if \[ \Vert v \Vert \leqslant p\,\vert x\vert. \]
\end{DoxyNote}
For matrices, the comparison is done using the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm. For this reason, the value of the reference scalar {\itshape other} should come from the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm of a reference matrix of same dimensions.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1dd502457286f60df1c3e90f9192c542}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!LinSpaced@{LinSpaced}}
\index{LinSpaced@{LinSpaced}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{LinSpaced()}{LinSpaced()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1dd502457286f60df1c3e90f9192c542} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Random\+Access\+Lin\+Spaced\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Lin\+Spaced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{low}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{high}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Sets a linearly spaced vector.    

The function generates \textquotesingle{}size\textquotesingle{} equally spaced values in the closed interval \mbox{[}low,high\mbox{]}. When size is set to 1, a vector of length 1 containing \textquotesingle{}high\textquotesingle{} is returned.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


For integer scalar types, an even spacing is possible if and only if the length of the range, i.\+e., {\ttfamily high-\/low} is a scalar multiple of {\ttfamily size-\/1}, or if {\ttfamily size} is a scalar multiple of the number of values {\ttfamily high-\/low+1} (meaning each value can be repeated the same number of time). If one of these two considions is not satisfied, then {\ttfamily high} is lowered to the largest value satisfying one of this constraint. Here are some examples\+:

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a52381e525a33db582d2dcbbac710e1d3} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int Na\+NPropagation$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1traits}{internal\+::traits}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{\+::\+Scalar}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::max\+Coeff (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the maximum of all coefficients of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}. In case {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} contains NaN, Na\+NPropagation determines the behavior\+: Na\+NPropagation == Propagate\+Fast \+: undefined Na\+NPropagation == Propagate\+NaN \+: result is NaN Na\+NPropagation == Propagate\+Numbers \+: result is maximum of elements that are not NaN 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
the matrix must be not empty, otherwise an assertion is triggered. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_affbd287191d45cf87dd419e77b7d3ff9} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int N$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1NColsBlockXpr}{NCols\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ N $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::middle\+Cols (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{n}{ = {\ttfamily N}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a block consisting of a range of columns of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em N} & the number of columns in the block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start\+Col} & the index of the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em n} & the number of columns in the block as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape n} should equal {\itshape N} unless {\itshape N} is {\itshape Dynamic}.

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a4ca170ba37a8def95cca1965aecce1d1}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!minCoeff@{minCoeff}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{minCoeff()}{minCoeff()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a4ca170ba37a8def95cca1965aecce1d1} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int Na\+NPropagation, typename Index\+Type$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1traits}{internal\+::traits}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{\+::\+Scalar}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::min\+Coeff (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Index\+Type \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{row\+Id}{, }\item[{Index\+Type \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{col\+Id}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the minimum of all coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this and puts in \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}row and \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}col its location.
\end{DoxyReturn}
In case {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} contains NaN, Na\+NPropagation determines the behavior\+: Na\+NPropagation == Propagate\+Fast \+: undefined Na\+NPropagation == Propagate\+NaN \+: result is NaN Na\+NPropagation == Propagate\+Numbers \+: result is maximum of elements that are not NaN \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
the matrix must be not empty, otherwise an assertion is triggered.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NullaryExpr()}{NullaryExpr()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ace7d7f3237fde5e1a5c82d36c93685be} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Custom\+Nullary\+Op$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1CwiseNullaryOp}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op}}$<$ Custom\+Nullary\+Op, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{\+::\+Plain\+Object}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Nullary\+Expr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{cols}{, }\item[{const Custom\+Nullary\+Op \&}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a matrix defined by a custom functor {\itshape func} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{classEigen_1_1MatrixBase}{Matrix\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Custom\+Nullary\+Op$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1CwiseNullaryOp}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op}}$<$ Custom\+Nullary\+Op, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{\+::\+Plain\+Object}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Nullary\+Expr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{size}{, }\item[{const Custom\+Nullary\+Op \&}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a matrix defined by a custom functor {\itshape func} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameter {\itshape size} is the size of the returned vector. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{classEigen_1_1MatrixBase}{Matrix\+Base} type.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size vector types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape size} as argument, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1CommaInitializer}{Comma\+Initializer}}$<$ Derived $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::operator$<$$<$ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{s}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_MatrixBaseCommaInitRef}%
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_MatrixBaseCommaInitRef}%
Convenient operator to set the coefficients of a matrix.

The coefficients must be provided in a row major order and exactly match the size of the matrix. Otherwise an assertion is raised.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
According the c++ standard, the argument expressions of this comma initializer are evaluated in arbitrary order.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a6462697d5a6fa3104f5f1213fdf9ff12} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::operator= (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1EigenBase}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies the generic expression {\itshape other} into \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this. 

The expression must provide a (templated) eval\+To(\+Derived\& dst) const function which does the actual job. In practice, this allows any user to write its own special matrix without having to modify \doxylink{classEigen_1_1MatrixBase}{Matrix\+Base}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a reference to \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1e002168ce504d56d923e54463ae6553}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!outerSize@{outerSize}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{outerSize()}{outerSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a1e002168ce504d56d923e54463ae6553} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+CONSTEXPR \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::outer\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the outer size.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For a vector, this returns just 1. For a matrix (non-\/vector), this is the major dimension with respect to the storage order, i.\+e., the number of columns for a column-\/major matrix, and the number of rows for a row-\/major matrix. 
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Random\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Random (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a fixed-\/size random matrix or vector expression
\end{DoxyReturn}
Numbers are uniformly spread through their whole definition range for integer types, and in the \mbox{[}-\/1\+:1\mbox{]} range for floating point scalar types.

This variant is only for fixed-\/size \doxylink{classEigen_1_1MatrixBase}{Matrix\+Base} types. For dynamic-\/size types, you need to use the variants taking size arguments.

Example\+:

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


This expression has the "{}evaluate before nesting"{} flag so that it will be evaluated into a temporary matrix whenever it is nested in a larger expression. This prevents unexpected behavior with expressions involving random matrices.

\textbackslash{}not\+\_\+reentrant

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ae97f8d9d08f969c733c8144be6225756}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!Random@{Random}}
\index{Random@{Random}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Random()}{Random()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ae97f8d9d08f969c733c8144be6225756} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Random\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Random (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a random matrix expression
\end{DoxyReturn}
Numbers are uniformly spread through their whole definition range for integer types, and in the \mbox{[}-\/1\+:1\mbox{]} range for floating point scalar types.

The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{classEigen_1_1MatrixBase}{Matrix\+Base} type.

\textbackslash{}not\+\_\+reentrant

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_ae814abb451b48ed872819192dc188c19}{Random()} should be used instead.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


This expression has the "{}evaluate before nesting"{} flag so that it will be evaluated into a temporary matrix whenever it is nested in a larger expression. This prevents unexpected behavior with expressions involving random matrices.

See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a4aed103f49b650b70bc9f34d96068832}{Dense\+Base\+::\+Nullary\+Expr(\+Index, const Custom\+Nullary\+Op\&)} for an example using C++11 random generators.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a539847ae1f9922a4f22ac918f0d03b29} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1traits}{internal\+::traits}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{\+::\+Scalar}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::redux (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Func \&}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the result of a full redux operation on the whole matrix or vector using {\itshape func} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The template parameter {\itshape Binary\+Op} is the type of the functor {\itshape func} which must be an associative operator. Both current C++98 and C++11 functor styles are handled.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
the matrix must be not empty, otherwise an assertion is triggered.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a13027a493a68a13496610caf3d81bd3e}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!resize@{resize}}
\index{resize@{resize}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resize()}{resize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a13027a493a68a13496610caf3d81bd3e} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{new\+Size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Only plain matrices/arrays, not expressions, may be resized; therefore the only useful resize methods are \doxylink{classEigen_1_1PlainObjectBase_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Matrix\+::resize()} and \doxylink{classEigen_1_1PlainObjectBase_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Array\+::resize()}. The present method only asserts that the new size equals the old size, and does nothing else. \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aef40c2ee48a85a799270c8258cc12b76}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!resize@{resize}}
\index{resize@{resize}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resize()}{resize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aef40c2ee48a85a799270c8258cc12b76} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Only plain matrices/arrays, not expressions, may be resized; therefore the only useful resize methods are \doxylink{classEigen_1_1PlainObjectBase_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Matrix\+::resize()} and \doxylink{classEigen_1_1PlainObjectBase_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Array\+::resize()}. The present method only asserts that the new size equals the old size, and does nothing else. \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acde1eef3a99bbbb4ac694ca55b1764c8}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!reverse@{reverse}}
\index{reverse@{reverse}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acde1eef3a99bbbb4ac694ca55b1764c8}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1Reverse}{Const\+Reverse\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::reverse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the const version of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acde1eef3a99bbbb4ac694ca55b1764c8}{reverse()}. \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a11014cd4565501e332bdd38c0028f736}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!reverseInPlace@{reverseInPlace}}
\index{reverseInPlace@{reverseInPlace}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{reverseInPlace()}{reverseInPlace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a11014cd4565501e332bdd38c0028f736} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::reverse\+In\+Place (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the "{}in place"{} version of reverse\+: it reverses {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.

In most cases it is probably better to simply use the reversed expression of a matrix. However, when reversing the matrix data itself is really needed, then this "{}in-\/place"{} version is probably the right choice because it provides the following additional benefits\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item less error prone\+: doing the same operation with .\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acde1eef3a99bbbb4ac694ca55b1764c8}{reverse()} requires special care\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{m\ =\ m.reverse().eval();\ }

\end{DoxyCode}

\item this API enables reverse operations without the need for a temporary
\item it allows future optimizations (cache friendliness, etc.)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1VectorwiseOp_a2bd419527acce58e9e813a5af654b81c}{Vectorwise\+Op\+::reverse\+In\+Place()}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acde1eef3a99bbbb4ac694ca55b1764c8}{reverse()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename NType$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedSegmentReturnType}{Fixed\+Segment\+Return\+Type}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NType $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8da735a6bfc7012606acf787156d10a0}{\+::value}} $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::segment (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{start}{, }\item[{NType}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

an expression of a segment (i.\+e. a vector block) in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.

\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of coefficients {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block() } for the details.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{setLinSpaced@{setLinSpaced}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLinSpaced()}{setLinSpaced()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a99dd31774d69545aba5d4f598cd27c4b} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::set\+Lin\+Spaced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{low}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{high}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets a linearly spaced vector. 

The function fills {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with equally spaced values in the closed interval \mbox{[}low,high\mbox{]}. When size is set to 1, a vector of length 1 containing \textquotesingle{}high\textquotesingle{} is returned.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

For integer scalar types, do not miss the explanations on the definition of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a513c7986f48517c36f992a558f81e591}{even spacing }.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a513c7986f48517c36f992a558f81e591}{Lin\+Spaced(\+Index,const Scalar\&,const Scalar\&)}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a17a69cfd1b44b64f26b1a0f00666a871}{set\+Lin\+Spaced(\+Index, const Scalar\&, const Scalar\&)}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1CwiseNullaryOp}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::set\+Lin\+Spaced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{new\+Size}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{low}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{high}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets a linearly spaced vector. 

The function generates \textquotesingle{}size\textquotesingle{} equally spaced values in the closed interval \mbox{[}low,high\mbox{]}. When size is set to 1, a vector of length 1 containing \textquotesingle{}high\textquotesingle{} is returned.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a39046dff78acbcb389ad0b018e587c8e} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::set\+Random (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Sets all coefficients in this expression to random values.

Numbers are uniformly spread through their whole definition range for integer types, and in the \mbox{[}-\/1\+:1\mbox{]} range for floating point scalar types.

\textbackslash{}not\+\_\+reentrant

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em N} & the number of coefficients in the segment as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape n} should equal {\itshape N} unless {\itshape N} is {\itshape Dynamic}.

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedSegmentReturnType}{Fixed\+Segment\+Return\+Type}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1get__fixed__value}{internal\+::get\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+value}}$<$ NType $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8da735a6bfc7012606acf787156d10a0}{\+::value}} $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::tail (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{NType}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a last coefficients of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with either dynamic or fixed sizes.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em NType} & the type of the value handling the number of coefficients in the segment, typically \doxylink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


The number of coefficients {\itshape n} can also be specified at compile-\/time by passing Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$, or Eigen\+::fix$<$\+N$>$(n) as arguments. See \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aea3e98d95cd47acce1bf5721f573ed70}{block() } for the details.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even in the case that the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$int CRows, int CCols$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1DenseBase_1_1FixedBlockXpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\+::\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::top\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a top-\/left corner of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Transpose\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::transpose (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of the transpose of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
If you want to replace a matrix by its own transpose, do {\bfseries{NOT}} do this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{m\ =\ m.transpose();\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ bug!!!\ caused\ by\ aliasing\ effect}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 Instead, use the \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a2bf1856f4ff79f0db0e6d416a2edfb0f}{transpose\+In\+Place()} method\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{m.transposeInPlace();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 which gives \doxylink{namespaceEigen}{Eigen} good opportunities for optimization, or alternatively you can also do\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{m\ =\ m.transpose().eval();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a2bf1856f4ff79f0db0e6d416a2edfb0f}{transpose\+In\+Place()}, adjoint() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aeedbef96d04a73342f6f62ec1a1c46e3}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!transpose@{transpose}}
\index{transpose@{transpose}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transpose()}{transpose()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_aeedbef96d04a73342f6f62ec1a1c46e3} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Const\+Transpose\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::transpose (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

This is the const version of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acdada00d813939c0c9e90db5c01585c8}{transpose()}.

Make sure you read the warning for \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acdada00d813939c0c9e90db5c01585c8}{transpose()} !

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a2bf1856f4ff79f0db0e6d416a2edfb0f}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!transposeInPlace@{transposeInPlace}}
\index{transposeInPlace@{transposeInPlace}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transposeInPlace()}{transposeInPlace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a2bf1856f4ff79f0db0e6d416a2edfb0f} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::transpose\+In\+Place (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the "{}in place"{} version of \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acdada00d813939c0c9e90db5c01585c8}{transpose()}\+: it replaces {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} by its own transpose. Thus, doing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{m.transposeInPlace();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 has the same effect on m as doing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{m\ =\ m.transpose().eval();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 and is faster and also safer because in the latter line of code, forgetting the \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} results in a bug caused by aliasing.

Notice however that this method is only useful if you want to replace a matrix by its own transpose. If you just need the transpose of a matrix, use \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acdada00d813939c0c9e90db5c01585c8}{transpose()}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
if the matrix is not square, then {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} must be a resizable matrix. This excludes (non-\/square) fixed-\/size matrices, block-\/expressions and maps.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_acdada00d813939c0c9e90db5c01585c8}{transpose()}, adjoint(), adjoint\+In\+Place() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a7f73df3954a09c7ab0dca208b6b23ddd}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!visit@{visit}}
\index{visit@{visit}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{visit()}{visit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a7f73df3954a09c7ab0dca208b6b23ddd} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Visitor$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::visit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Visitor \&}]{visitor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Applies the visitor {\itshape visitor} to the whole coefficients of the matrix or vector.

The template parameter {\itshape Visitor} is the type of the visitor and provides the following interface\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }MyVisitor\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ called\ for\ the\ first\ coefficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ init(\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ Scalar\&\ value,\ Index\ i,\ Index\ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ called\ for\ all\ other\ coefficients}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ operator()\ (\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ Scalar\&\ value,\ Index\ i,\ Index\ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
compared to one or two {\itshape for} {\itshape loops}, visitors offer automatic unrolling for small fixed size matrix.

if the matrix is empty, then the visitor is left unchanged.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
min\+Coeff(\+Index\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*},\+Index\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}), max\+Coeff(\+Index\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*},\+Index\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}), Dense\+Base\+::redux() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a3832aa9b2ee9ebdb4458003c742c9027} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Zero (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an expression of a zero matrix.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{classEigen_1_1MatrixBase}{Matrix\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size vector types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape size} as argument, so \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a3806d3f42de165878dace160e6aba40a} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
std\+::ostream \& operator$<$$<$ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::ostream \&}]{s}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$ \&}]{m}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [related]}}

Outputs the matrix, to the given stream.

If you wish to print the matrix with a format different than the default, use \doxylink{classEigen_1_1DenseBase_a148e20e32aa3ceca13e0a49c2cc584fc}{Dense\+Base\+::format()}.

It is also possible to change the default format by defining EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+IO\+\_\+\+FORMAT before including \doxylink{namespaceEigen}{Eigen} headers. If not defined, this will automatically be defined to \doxylink{structEigen_1_1IOFormat}{Eigen\+::\+IOFormat()}, that is the \doxylink{structEigen_1_1IOFormat}{Eigen\+::\+IOFormat} with default parameters.
